Entering into the house you walk right into the Living Room of the house where we have a massive window from floor to ceiling with sliding doors that lead to the spacious deck. In the Living room we have 2 comfortable leather couches placed in front of the indoor fireplace. We have a full kitchen equipped with all utensils, plates and pots and pans. This entry level has two bedrooms, the first bedroom has a full sized bed, the second bedroom has two twin beds. Both Bedrooms have their own closet and plenty of storage space. This level also has a full bathroom with marble walls, and a bath tub. Upstairs we have the master bedroom, it has its own deck and balcony and half bathroom. The Master bedroom has a temperdic mattress with a beautiful zen framed bed. It has a seating area and plenty of closet space. Prior to the entrance of the master bedroom we have a loft area with a futon that can be unfolded to sleep on.
The cabin comes equipped with a washer and dryer, central heating system, refrigerator, stove, oven, microwave, toaster, coffee maker and a wifi. Sheets and towels are provided as well. We do not have TV because we wish for guests to instead enjoy the surrounding nature and the friends and family that join on the trip.
On a side note, in regards to kids and infants, stairs to the upstairs master bedroom only has a banister(handrail) on one side (the wall side). The other side of the stairs is open so parents please be aware of this, in addition the loft on the master bedroom level has guardrails that are wide meaning that very small kids could squeeze through, we ask that parents please be aware of this for the safety of your kids.

springs. You’ll love my place because its clean, cute, dreamy and right across from the best hiking trail ever!  The room is good for couples, solo adventurers, business travelers, and furry friends (pets).</div><div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1293">The Dreamy room includes a full sized mattress - super comfy with a down comforter!  The bathroom is shared with one other guest room. There are two bedrooms on the third floor. Shampoo is always included as well as clean towels and sheets.  Your room has a desk, hangers in the closet, drawers to store your things, a built in vanity, and stunning views of the mountains. We are a 420 friendly home. If you're offended by this beware! 

Step outside the house onto the courtyard to eat breakfast amongst the trees.  There is even a fountain out there, ask me how to turn it on!

Across the street from the house is a hiking trail that goes for miles and miles. You don't even have to get in your car to hike! Lake Gregory is a 10 minute walk from the house as well as the grocery store and tons of cute antique shops. Lake Arrowhead and Big Bear are both a short (and incredibly stunning) drive away.

Pets:
We have two dogs -  mine is a german shepherd / Golden retriever mix.  He's generally friendly but very protective of the house and tends to bark when guests first arrive, but immediately stops as soon as you say hi to him.  He is friendly to other dogs as well.  My roommate also has a dog, a pure bred german shepherd,  Very friendly as well! 

Shared Space:
Please be aware that the house is shared!  Your room is private but the kitchen, living room and patios are all shared with other guests and myself.  I'm usually home, but on occasion i go out of town and rent these rooms, ill let you know if that is the case.   Currently living here:  Myself and my boyfriend in the basement, and a roommate named Jeff across the hall from this room.  He is a music producer, you might hear him making music in the day, but don't worry his stuff is very beautiful and ethereal.  Nothing loud and obnoxious! 

Parking:
You can park in the dirt area across the street.  If you see space in the driveway please be sure not to take up the entire driveway.  If we all park smart three cars can fit in there. 

Disclaimer:
If you are offended by black walls, astrology, tarot cards, crystals, and mystical artwork etc please do not stay here.  We are very open minded, positive energy people.
